## Organizational information

### Organization

[Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order")[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_I-1)

### Position type

Jedi rank[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_I-1)

### Duties

* To train a [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") in the ways of the [light side of the Force](/wiki/Light_side_of_the_Force "Light side of the Force")[[2]](#cite_note-TSWB-2)
* [Jedi General](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General") (during the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"))[[3]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-3)

[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:TitleOrPosition)

:   "*Heeded my words not, did you? Pass on what you have learned. Strength, mastery. But weakness… folly… failure, also. Yes, failure most of all. The greatest teacher, failure is. Luke… we are what they grow beyond. That is the true burden of all masters.*"
:   ―Yoda's Force spirit, to Luke Skywalker[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_8-4)

**Jedi Master** was a rank in the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") given to wise and powerful [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi"), many of whom were prominent leaders within the Order.

Only Masters were allowed to serve on the [Jedi High Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council "Jedi High Council"). A notable exception to this, however, was when [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") was appointed to the Council as a representative of [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") [Sheev Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") despite only being a [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight").

## Description[]

:   "*Those who have undertaken the most serious study and hold the deepest devotion to the Force will achieve the rank of Jedi Master. It is more than just an honorary title, for upon achieving the rank of Master, the Order expects a Jedi to forge their own path and pursue independent studies. However, some masters might still take a Padawan, or return to the Grand Temple to educate younglings. Masters are also eligible to be named to the Grand Council as leaders of the Order. For a very select few, the title of Grand Master awaits only the most illustrious among us.*"
:   ―Jedi Master [Harli Cogra](/wiki/Harli_Cogra "Harli Cogra")[[5]](#cite_note-Chronicles_of_the_Jedi-5)

 [![Yoda was both a Jedi Master and Grand Master of the Jedi Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e8/Yoda_ME.png/revision/latest?cb=20181129025756) [![Yoda was both a Jedi Master and Grand Master of the Jedi Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e8/Yoda_ME.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20181129025756)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e8/Yoda_ME.png/revision/latest?cb=20181129025756) 

Yoda was both a Jedi Master and Grand Master of the Jedi Order.

 

A [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") Master was a [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") who had been offered a higher ranking within [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") as a result of a Jedi [Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master "Grand Master") seeing the Knight fit for the position.[[2]](#cite_note-TSWB-2) Compared to a Knight, a Jedi Master had greater experience, greater readiness, and had shown their devotion to taking their next step as part of the Order: to be a Jedi Master was the next rank all Jedi Knights worked towards as part of their life-long devotion to studying [The Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force"), but it was a long road to prove oneself worthy of the title.[[6]](#cite_note-Convergence-6) Upon being given the rank, the Jedi Master was able to and expected to pursue their own studies, moving forward in their experience with [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force") on their own terms. In fact, the [Jedi High Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council "Jedi High Council") outright expected all Jedi Masters to do so.[[7]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-7)

There were several ways for a Jedi Knight to be promoted into a Jedi Master. One way was for the Knight to successfully train [Padawans](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan"), passing on their knowledge of [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force")[[8]](#cite_note-Insider_199-8) in order to ensure the Order survived into the next generation.[[3]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-3) Alternatively, a Jedi Knight could prove themself in battle.[[8]](#cite_note-Insider_199-8) In general, those who were offered the rank of Master had undertaken serious study and held a deep loyalty to the Force.[[5]](#cite_note-Chronicles_of_the_Jedi-5) When the moment called for a serious response, Jedi Masters were expected to be serious instead of acting glib.[[9]](#cite_note-Kanan_7-9) Often groups of [Jedi younglings](/wiki/Jedi_Initiate "Jedi Initiate") would receive their early education in the ways of the Force under the guidance of a single Jedi Master. The [younglings](/wiki/Youngling "Youngling") would then receive more direct [training](/wiki/Jedi_training "Jedi training") under the direction from either a Jedi Knight or a Jedi Master.[[2]](#cite_note-TSWB-2) Jedi Masters and Jedi Knights served as Jedi Generals in the [Republic Military](/wiki/Republic_Military "Republic Military") during the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars") while [Padawans](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") served as [Jedi Commanders](/wiki/Jedi_Commander "Jedi Commander").[[3]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-3)

## History[]

:   "*The title of Jedi Master was bestowed upon the most powerful members of the Jedi Order.*"
:   ―Luke Skywalker[[10]](#cite_note-Star_Wars:_The_Secrets_of_the_Jedi-10)

 [![Jedi Master ](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/KelleranBeqBalance-ABig.png/revision/latest?cb=20200604144818) [![Jedi Master ](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/KelleranBeqBalance-ABig.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200604144818)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/KelleranBeqBalance-ABig.png/revision/latest?cb=20200604144818) 

Jedi Master [Kelleran Beq](/wiki/Kelleran_Beq "Kelleran Beq")

 

In the time of the [High Republic](/wiki/High_Republic_Era "High Republic Era"), the Jedi High Council notably consisted of three Jedi Grand Masters; [Xo Lahru](/wiki/Xo_Lahru "Xo Lahru"), [Pra-Tre Veter](/wiki/Pra-Tre_Veter "Pra-Tre Veter"), and [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda") all elected to share the role. Other masters of High [Republic Era](/wiki/Republic_Era "Republic Era") included [Jora Malli](/wiki/Jora_Malli "Jora Malli"), [Stellan Gios](/wiki/Stellan_Gios "Stellan Gios"), [Sskeer](/wiki/Sskeer "Sskeer"), [Oppo Rancisis](/wiki/Oppo_Rancisis "Oppo Rancisis"), [Yarael Poof](/wiki/Yarael_Poof "Yarael Poof"), and [Avar Kriss](/wiki/Avar_Kriss "Avar Kriss").[[7]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-7) [Ry Ki-Sakka](/wiki/Ry_Ki-Sakka "Ry Ki-Sakka") also gained the Grand Master rank at some point.[[11]](#cite_note-THRS_4-11) As one of the oldest Jedi Masters in the order's history, Yoda,[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_V-12) over the course of his 800-[year](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year")-long career as a Jedi Master, trained no fewer than 20,000 Jedi[[13]](#cite_note-AEYTK-13) and held the position of Jedi Grand Master for over 800 years.[[14]](#cite_note-DatabankYoda-14)

In the years of the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic"), the Jedi High Council was made up of twelve Jedi Masters, one which bore the title of Grand Master,[[15]](#cite_note-sweJO-15) who had the power to grant Jedi Knights the title of Master, in consensus. Other prominent Jedi Masters who also sat on the Council included members, such as [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu"), [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi"), [Kit Fisto](/wiki/Kit_Fisto "Kit Fisto"), [Adi Gallia](/wiki/Adi_Gallia "Adi Gallia"), [Yaddle](/wiki/Yaddle "Yaddle"), [Saesee Tiin](/wiki/Saesee_Tiin "Saesee Tiin"), [Agen Kolar](/wiki/Agen_Kolar "Agen Kolar"), [Even Piell](/wiki/Even_Piell "Even Piell"), and [Shaak Ti](/wiki/Shaak_Ti "Shaak Ti").[[16]](#cite_note-Episode_III-16) Many Jedi Masters also took on apprentices to train in the ways of the Force, such as [Depa Billaba](/wiki/Depa_Billaba "Depa Billaba")[[17]](#cite_note-A_New_Dawn-17) and [Luminara Unduli](/wiki/Luminara_Unduli "Luminara Unduli").[[18]](#cite_note-Weapons_Factory-18)

 [![During the Clone Wars, Jedi Masters held the rank of Jedi General over clone troopers in the Republic Military.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Wolfpack_Felucia.png/revision/latest?cb=20130530015004) [![During the Clone Wars, Jedi Masters held the rank of Jedi General over clone troopers in the Republic Military.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Wolfpack_Felucia.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20130530015004)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Wolfpack_Felucia.png/revision/latest?cb=20130530015004) 

During the Clone Wars, Jedi Masters held the rank of Jedi General over clone troopers in the Republic Military.

 

Under the [Jedi Military Integration Act](/wiki/Jedi_Military_Integration_Act "Jedi Military Integration Act"), Jedi Masters and Jedi Knights were given the rank of Jedi General for the Clone Wars.[[19]](#cite_note-Brotherhood-19) After serving as a Jedi Knight for three years during the war, [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") advanced to the point in his training that he felt he deserved the rank of Jedi Master, though the Council did not agree. When [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") [Sheev Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") appointed Skywalker to the Council as his personal representative, the Council reluctantly agreed, hoping to use him as a means to [spy](/wiki/Spy "Spy") on Palpatine. However, the Council did not grant Skywalker the title of Master. Skywalker took this as both an outrageous and unfair insult, as no Jedi in the history of the Jedi Order had ever been placed on the Council without receiving the rank of Master.[[16]](#cite_note-Episode_III-16)

Years after the [Great Jedi Purge](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge") and the [Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War"), [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker") attempted to train his own generation of Jedi and was considered a Jedi Master.[[20]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-20)[[21]](#cite_note-21) Following the [Battle of Exegol](/wiki/Battle_of_Exegol "Battle of Exegol") in [35 ABY](/wiki/35_ABY "35 ABY"),[[22]](#cite_note-TROS_Date-22) [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker") took up the [family name](/wiki/Skywalker_family "Skywalker family") of her mentors Luke Skywalker and[[2]](#cite_note-TSWB-2) [Leia Skywalker Organa Solo](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo").[[23]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-23) Now the last Jedi, Rey Skywalker eventually ascended to the rank of Master.[[2]](#cite_note-TSWB-2)

## Behind the scenes[]

As confirmed by editor [Tom Hoeler](/wiki/Tom_Hoeler "Tom Hoeler"), the word "master" in "Jedi Master" must be capitalized if used with "Jedi." The word "master" on its own, however, does not always need to be capitalized.[[24]](#cite_note-Jedi_Master_Tom-24) "Master Jedi," meanwhile, is an honorific used among certain cultures or by certain individuals, rather than a reference to the "Jedi Master" rank itself.[[25]](#cite_note-Jedi_Master_Tom_2-25)

[↑](#cite_ref-sweJO_15-0) [StarWars.com Encyclopedia](/wiki/Encyclopedia_(StarWars.com) "StarWars.com Encyclopedia") [Jedi Order](https://web.archive.org/web/20131227172722/http://starwars.com/explore/encyclopedia/groups/jediorder) in the [Encyclopedia](/wiki/Encyclopedia_(StarWars.com) "Encyclopedia (StarWars.com)") ([original site](http://starwars.com/explore/encyclopedia/groups/jediorder) is defunct) 16. ↑ [16.0](#cite_ref-Episode_III_16-0) [16.1](#cite_ref-Episode_III_16-1) [*Star Wars*: Episode III *Revenge of the Sith*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_III_Revenge_of_the_Sith "Star Wars: Episode III Revenge of the Sith") 17. [↑](#cite_ref-A_New_Dawn_17-0) [*A New Dawn*](/wiki/A_New_Dawn_(novel) "A New Dawn (novel)") 18. [↑](#cite_ref-Weapons_Factory_18-0) [TCW mini logo](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: The Clone Wars") *[Star Wars: The Clone Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: The Clone Wars")* — "[Weapons Factory](/wiki/Weapons_Factory "Weapons Factory")" 19. [↑](#cite_ref-Brotherhood_19-0) [*Brotherhood*](/wiki/Brotherhood_(novel) "Brotherhood (novel)") 20. [↑](#cite_ref-Episode_VII_20-0) [*Star Wars*: Episode VII *The Force Awakens*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_VII_The_Force_Awakens "Star Wars: Episode VII The Force Awakens") 21. [↑](#cite_ref-21) *[The Secrets of the Jedi](/wiki/The_Secrets_of_the_Jedi "The Secrets of the Jedi")* 22. [↑](#cite_ref-TROS_Date_22-0) *[Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Skywalker:_The_Visual_Dictionary "Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary")* dates the events of *Star Wars*: Episode IX *The Rise of Skywalker* as taking place one [year](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") after the [Starkiller Incident](/wiki/Hosnian_Cataclysm "Hosnian Cataclysm"), which *[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galactic_Atlas "Star Wars: Galactic Atlas")* dates to [34 ABY](/wiki/34_ABY "34 ABY"). Therefore, the events of *Star Wars*: Episode IX *The Rise of Skywalker* must take place in [35 ABY](/wiki/35_ABY "35 ABY"). 23. [↑](#cite_ref-TROS_EE_23-0) *[Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: Expanded Edition](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Skywalker:_Expanded_Edition "Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: Expanded Edition")* 24. [↑](#cite_ref-Jedi_Master_Tom_24-0) [TwitterLogo](https://twitter.com) [Tom Hoeler](/wiki/Tom_Hoeler "Tom Hoeler") ([@DarthInternous](https://twitter.com/DarthInternous)) on [Twitter](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Twitter "wikipedia:Twitter") ([post](https://twitter.com/DarthInternous/status/1770107828499271783)): "Master should always be capitalized when used in combination with the word Jedi. Master on its own does not always require capitalization." ([backup link](https://archive.ph/j92WB)) 25. [↑](#cite_ref-Jedi_Master_Tom_2_25-0) [TwitterLogo](https://twitter.com) [Tom Hoeler](/wiki/Tom_Hoeler "Tom Hoeler") ([@DarthInternous](https://twitter.com/DarthInternous)) on [Twitter](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Twitter "wikipedia:Twitter") ([post](https://twitter.com/DarthInternous/status/1770313258920038481)): "Jedi is a singular plural, so Jedi is always Jedi. Master Jedi is usually an honorific used by certain beings and cultures, and as such would be capitalized because it is a referrant. (In response to: "But should it be Master Jedis or Jedi masters?")" ([backup link](https://archive.ph/TD7RO)) |
